                                BEGIN
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.SetPurchInvHeader(dPurchInvHeader);

                                  mTitle := STRSUBSTNO(tTitle, dPurchInvHeader."No.");

                                  lFormatAddress.Company(mCompanyAddress, mCompanyInformation);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchInvBuyFrom(mBuyFromAddress, dPurchInvHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchInvPayTo(mPayToAddress, dPurchInvHeader);
                                  lFormatAddress.PurchInvShipTo(mShipToAddress, dPurchInvHeader);

                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.ContactInformation(mBuyFromContact);
                                  mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.CurrencyInformation(mCurrencyText, mCurrencyFactorText, mAmountText, mAmountInclVatText);

                                  mPurchaserText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.SalespersonPurchaserText();
                                  mPaymentTermsText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.PaymentTermsText();
                                  mPaymentMethodText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.PaymentMethodText();
                                  mShipmentMethodText := mPurchasePrintoutToolkit.ShipmentMethodText();
                                END;
                                 }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
